## Instruction

Today we have 3 new employees joining us, and each employee's information is stored in the Snowflake database.

Based on the employee's group assignment and training manual, automatically generate training task lists, send emails to the employee's email address, and update the task content and planned completion dates to the database.

For new employees, send onboarding emails in the following format:

```
Dear xxx, You have the following training tasks to complete:
xxx
xxx
xxx
Please complete them as soon as possible.
```

Additionally, you need to check for employee records where the current date has exceeded the training completion deadline but the task status is still "incomplete", send reminder emails to the employees themselves in the same format.

The order of the tasks in the email should be based on the order in the training manual.

And remember to CC their direct supervisor.

## Initial State

### Snowflake

You can view the database build process [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/finalpool_dev/tasks/finalpool/landing-task-reminder/preprocess).

<Expandable title="Details">
```json arguments
{
	"query": "SELECT \n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	\n    e.NAME,
	\n    e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	\n    s.NAME as SUPERVISOR_NAME,
	\n    CASE \n        WHEN EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_DATA gtd WHERE gtd.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID) THEN 'DATA'\n        WHEN EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_BACKEND gtb WHERE gtb.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID) THEN 'BACKEND'\n        WHEN EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_FRONTEND gtf WHERE gtf.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID) THEN 'FRONTEND'\n        WHEN EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_TESTING gtt WHERE gtt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID) THEN 'TESTING'\n        ELSE 'NONE'\n    END as GROUP_ASSIGNMENT\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE s ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = s.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE e.EMPLOYEE_ID BETWEEN 6001 AND 6020\nORDER BY e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	 e.EMPLOYEE_ID"
}

```

- Supervisor 8001 (Jennifer Baker) → BACKEND group
- Supervisor 8002 (Victoria Jackson) → FRONTEND group  
- Supervisor 8003 (Debra Rogers) → TESTING group
- Supervisor 8004 (Marie Green) → DATA group

So the new employees should be assigned as follows:
- 9001 (Dorothy Edwards) → BACKEND (reports to 8001 - Jennifer Baker)
- 9002 (Anthony Young) → FRONTEND (reports to 8002 - Victoria Jackson)

```json arguments
	 DDL\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_TESTING\nWHERE EMPLOYEE_ID = 9003\nORDER BY TASK_TYPE,
	 TASK_NAME"
}

```

```json arguments
{
	"query": "-- Find employees with overdue public tasks\nSELECT \n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	\n    e.NAME,
	\n    e.EMAIL,
	\n    s.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    pt.TASK_NAME,
	\n    pt.DDL,
	\n    DATEDIFF(day,
	 pt.DDL,
	 '2025-10-18') as DAYS_OVERDUE\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.PUBLIC_TASKS pt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON pt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE s ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = s.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE pt.DDL < '2025-10-18' \nAND pt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\nORDER BY e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 pt.TASK_NAME"
}

```

```json arguments
{
	"query": "-- Find employees with overdue group-specific tasks (Backend)\nSELECT \n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	\n    e.NAME,
	\n    e.EMAIL,
	\n    s.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    gt.TASK_NAME,
	\n    gt.DDL,
	\n    DATEDIFF(day,
	 gt.DDL,
	 '2025-10-18') as DAYS_OVERDUE,
	\n    'BACKEND' as TASK_GROUP\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_BACKEND gt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE s ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = s.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE gt.DDL < '2025-10-18' \nAND gt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n\nUNION ALL\n\n-- Find employees with overdue group-specific tasks (Frontend)\nSELECT \n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	\n    e.NAME,
	\n    e.EMAIL,
	\n    s.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    gt.TASK_NAME,
	\n    gt.DDL,
	\n    DATEDIFF(day,
	 gt.DDL,
	 '2025-10-18') as DAYS_OVERDUE,
	\n    'FRONTEND' as TASK_GROUP\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_FRONTEND gt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE s ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = s.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE gt.DDL < '2025-10-18' \nAND gt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n\nUNION ALL\n\n-- Find employees with overdue group-specific tasks (Testing)\nSELECT \n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	\n    e.NAME,
	\n    e.EMAIL,
	\n    s.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    gt.TASK_NAME,
	\n    gt.DDL,
	\n    DATEDIFF(day,
	 gt.DDL,
	 '2025-10-18') as DAYS_OVERDUE,
	\n    'TESTING' as TASK_GROUP\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_TESTING gt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE s ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = s.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE gt.DDL < '2025-10-18' \nAND gt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n\nUNION ALL\n\n-- Find employees with overdue group-specific tasks (Data)\nSELECT \n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	\n    e.NAME,
	\n    e.EMAIL,
	\n    s.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    gt.TASK_NAME,
	\n    gt.DDL,
	\n    DATEDIFF(day,
	 gt.DDL,
	 '2025-10-18') as DAYS_OVERDUE,
	\n    'DATA' as TASK_GROUP\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_DATA gt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE s ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = s.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE gt.DDL < '2025-10-18' \nAND gt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n\nORDER BY EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 TASK_NAME"
}

```
